The rational term $\frac{c A^2}{d A^4 + 1}$ is the key challenging piece. Let me check which candidates could reproduce this.

No rational function of the right form.

The rational piece is $(A+c_3)^{-2}$, degree 2 denominator. Not enough.

None of the candidates have an explicit $A^2/(A^4 + c)$ rational term. But could any reproduce it through other means?

**Candidate 33**: $A^{c_0} c_1 + c_2 \tanh(c_3 t + c_4) + c_5 \exp(c_6 t) + c_7 \log(A^{c_8} c_9 + 1)$

Let me reconsider: Could $\exp(A \cdot c)$ approximate the rational function? No — we need exact equivalence for all A.

**Candidate 41**: Rational functions in $t$ with polynomial dependence on $A$. This is $\frac{\text{polynomial in } A, t}{c_1 + t^2}$ structure. The GT has no such denominator in $t$.

Let me check if any candidate has a term like $A^2/(A^4 c + c)$ or equivalent. Looking through all 50 candidates... none of them contain a term with $A^4$ in a denominator or any structure that could yield $A^2/(A^4 + \text{const})$.
